<script language="javascript">
var topicId = "TNjA3Ng==";
var pageId = "TMjUyMDg=";



var BDECPager = function(config){
	this.data = [];
	this.pagenow = -1;
	this.pagetotal = 0;
	this.perpage = parseInt(config.perpage);
	this.pagehost = document.getElementById(config.domid);	
	if(this.pagehost){ this.init(); }
}
BDECPager.prototype = {
	init: function(){
		this.dom = {};	
		var divs = this.pagehost.getElementsByTagName('div');
		for(var i=0, len=divs.length; i<len; i++){
			var div = divs[i];
			if(div.className && div.className == 'items'){
				this.dom.items = div;
				break;
			}
		}
		if(!this.dom.items){ return; }
		var uls = this.dom.items.getElementsByTagName('ul');
		for(var i=0, len=uls.length; i<len; i++){
			var ul = uls[i];
			if(ul.className && ul.className == 'item'){
				this.data.push(ul);	
			}
		}
		if(!this.data.length){ return; }
		
		this.dom.pager = document.createElement('div'); 
		this.dom.pager.className = 'qPage';
		this.dom.pager_stat = document.createElement('div');
		this.dom.pager_stat.className = 'stat';
		this.dom.pager_turn = document.createElement('div');
		this.dom.pager_turn.className = 'turn';
		this.dom.pager_prev = document.createElement('div');
		this.dom.pager_prev.className = 'pre pre_disabled';
		this.dom.pager_next = document.createElement('div');
		this.dom.pager_next.className = 'next next_disabled';
		
		this.dom.pager_turn.appendChild(this.dom.pager_prev);
		this.dom.pager_turn.appendChild(this.dom.pager_next);
		this.dom.pager.appendChild(this.dom.pager_stat);
		this.dom.pager.appendChild(this.dom.pager_turn);
		this.pagehost.appendChild(this.dom.pager);
		this.pagetotal = Math.ceil(this.data.length/this.perpage);		
		this.isde = this.data.length%this.perpage == 0 ? true : false; //最后一页满
		this.bind();
	},
	bind: function(){
		var _this = this;
		if(this.pagetotal == 0){ return; }
		if(this.pagetotal > 1){
		this.dom.pager_prev.className = 'pre'; 
		this.dom.pager_prev.innerHTML = '<a href="#;"></a>';
		this.dom.pager_next.className = 'next'; 
		this.dom.pager_next.innerHTML = '<a href="#"></a>';		
		this.dom.pager_prev.getElementsByTagName('A')[0].onclick = function(){ _this.show(_this.pagenow - 1); return false; }
		this.dom.pager_next.getElementsByTagName('A')[0].onclick = function(){ _this.show(_this.pagenow + 1); return false; }
		}
		function randompager(pagetotal, isde){
			if(pagetotal == 1){ 
				return 1; 
			}
			var pagenum = parseInt(Math.random()*pagetotal) + 1;
			if(isde){ 
				return pagenum; 
			}else{
				if(pagenum != pagetotal){
					return pagenum;	
				}else{
					return randompager(pagetotal, isde);
				}
			}
		}
		var radomnum = randompager(this.pagetotal, this.isde)
		this.show(radomnum);
	},
	show: function(num){
		if(num == this.pagenow){ return; }
		else if(num > this.pagetotal){ num = 1; }
		else if(num < 1){ num = this.pagetotal; }
		//clear nodes
		while(this.dom.items.firstChild){
			this.dom.items.firstChild.parentNode.removeChild(this.dom.items.firstChild)
		}
		var start = (num-1)*this.perpage;
		var end = num*this.perpage;
		for(var i= start; i<end; i++){
			if(this.data[i]){
				this.data[i].style.display = 'block';
				this.dom.items.appendChild(this.data[i]);	
			}
		}
		this.dom.pager_stat.innerHTML = num + '/' + this.pagetotal;
		this.pagenow = num;	
		return false;
	}
}


window.nova_init_hook_adbanner = function() {
	if((navigator.userAgent.indexOf('iPod') != -1) || (navigator.userAgent.indexOf('iPad') != -1) || (navigator.userAgent.indexOf('iPhone') != -1))
	{
		var adVHolder = document.getElementById('ab_173');
		adVHolder.innerHTML = '<a style="display:block;width:300px;height:245px;margin:0 auto;" href="http://www.soku.com" target="_blank"><img src="http://res.mfs.ykimg.com/051000004F16874E97927318530CEC09.jpg" width="300" height="245" /></a>';
            
                 var adBHolder = document.getElementById('ab_407');
                 if(adBHolder.innerHTML == '')
                 {

}
